***фура.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фура.html>фу́ра</a> (18800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fuhre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фура.html>фу́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фура.html>фу́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фура.html>фу́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фура.html>фу́р</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> large, long cart</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wagon</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> van</li>
<li>semi-trailer truck, heavy vehicle</li></ol>

***фуражка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жка</a> (3392)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">forage cap</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg/220px-Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg" decoding="async" width="220" height="291" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg/330px-Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg/440px-Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg 2x" data-file-width="781" data-file-height="1033" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жка</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">furážka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">British</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> peaked cap, combination cap, forage cap</li>

***фургон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́н</a> (5106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fourgon</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">furgón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>portable loading room, van, caravan, wagon, waggon, camion <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a covered vehicle used for carrying goods</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b> December 29,  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корова.html>коро́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбежать.html>сбежа́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> скотобо́йни <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:вегетарианский.html>вегетариа́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рай.html>рай</a>»</span>”, in  <cite>Lenta.ru</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://lenta.ru/news/2018/12/29/cow/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сша.html>Сша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корова.html>коро́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самостоятельный.html>самостоя́тельно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбраться.html>вы́бралась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грузовик.html>грузовика́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вёзший.html>вёзшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> скотобо́йню, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбежать.html>сбежа́ла</a>.</span></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">V SŠA koróva samostojátelʹno výbralasʹ iz <b>furgóna</b> gruzoviká, vezševo živótnyx na skotobójnju, i sbežála.</span></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In the USA a cow got out of the <b>waggon</b> of a lorry that delivered animals to slaughter, and fled.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***фыркать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фыркать.html>фы́ркать</a> (11140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркать.html>фы́ркать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fýrkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркнуть.html>фы́ркнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to snort, to sniff</li>
<li>to sniff scornfully, to scoff, to grouse, to grumble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chuckle, to chortle, to snicker</li></ol>

***фыркнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фыркнуть.html>фы́ркнуть</a> (7705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркать.html>фы́ркать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fýrkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркнуть.html>фы́ркнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fýrknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фыркать.html>фы́ркать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to snort, to sniff</li>
<li>to sniff scornfully, to scoff, to grouse, to grumble</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chuckle, to chortle, to snicker</li></ol>

***хаживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хаживать.html>ха́живать</a> (25928)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хаживать.html>ха́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xáživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go somewhere, to visit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">repeatedly or frequently</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a>. П. Авенариус, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:бродящий.html>Бродя́щие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:современный.html>Совреме́нная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идиллия.html>иди́ллия</a></i> 1865:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хаживать.html>ха́живал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>не́ю</a> ― <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрекаться.html>отрека́юсь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хаживать.html>ха́живать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухаживать.html>уха́живать</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što ja <b>xážival</b> s néju ― ne otrekájusʹ, no <b>xáživatʹ</b> dalekó ješčó ne znáčit uxáživatʹ</i></dd><dd>I do not deny that I <b>visited</b> her, but <b>visiting</b> does not mean wooing</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is an iterative verb, and in standard language is conjugated only in the infinitive and the past tense.</li></ul>

***халат.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́т</a> (2126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">خلعت</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hilat</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">kaftan</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Azerbaijani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Azerbaijani language">Azerbaijani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="az">xələt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dressing gown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uzbek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Uzbek language">Uzbek</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="uz">xalat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">robe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">خِلْعَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḵilʿa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">robe of honor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xalát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dressing gown, bathrobe (for men or women)</li>

<li>oriental robe</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:халатик.html>хала́тик</a> (12102)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xalát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***халтура.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ра</a> (16893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">chartularius</i>, relating to a chartulary (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хартула́рий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xartulárij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> privy to the imparting of additional earnings. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">хавту́ра</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xavtúra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">хавту́р</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xavtúr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gift to clerics in kind; gift; graft, palm-oil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">хаўту́ры</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xaŭtúry</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">funeral</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xaltúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́р</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional<span class="ib-comma">,</span> now largely unknown</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> funeral banquet, extra-treats in connection to someone being interred
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1872</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Pavel_Ivanovich_Melnikov" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:en:Pavel Ivanovich Melnikov">андре́й пече́рскій</a>,  “Въ лѣса́хъ”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:The_Russian_Messenger" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:en:The Russian Messenger">ру́сскій вѣ́стникъ</a></cite>, volume 98, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=zvsYAAAAYAAJamp;pg=PA281">page 281</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Въ <a href = vnd.unilang:поминальный.html>помина́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дни</a> оби́тельски <a href = vnd.unilang:ворот.html>во́рота</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широко́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крещеный.html>крещёный</a> міръ, <a href = vnd.unilang:распахнутый.html>распа́хнуты</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>приди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сильный.html>си́льный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>приди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:немощный.html>не́мощный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>приди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:богатый.html>бога́тый</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>приди́</a> убо́гій — <a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́кому</a> мѣ́сто <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> столо́м … сберу́тся <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ру</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> „сиро́ты” <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́тери</a> съ бѣли́цами изъ захуда́лыхъ <a href = vnd.unilang:обитель.html>оби́телей</a>, приду́тъ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> дереве́нскіе христолю́бцы … <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́та</a> свои́хъ сро́дниковъ <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чужи́хъ харча́хъ <a href = vnd.unilang:помянуть.html>помяну́ть</a>?</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V pominálʹnyje dni obítelʹski vorota širokó, na vesʹ kreščónyj mir, raspáxnuty — pridí sílʹnyj, pridí némoščnyj, pridí bogátyj, pridí ubógij — vsjákomu mě́sto za stolóm … Sberútsja na <b>xaltúru</b> i „siróty” i máteri s bělícami iz zaxudályx obítelej, pridút i derevénskije xristoljúbcy … Komú ne oxóta svoíx sródnikov na čužíx xarčáx pomjanútʹ?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In funeral days the monasterial doors are flung open widely, to all the christened word – it may come the strong, it may come the powerless, it may come the wretched – to everyone there is a place before the table … to the <b>banquet</b> gather even the “orphans” and mothers with nuns from the abandoned cloisters, come even the rural Christ-lovers … Who does not want to commemorate his relatives on someone else’s catering?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминки.html>поми́нки</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pomínki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> yields acquired or work performed irregularly, job of imperfect compliance
<ol><li>undeclared work, black market job, supplementary contract, moonlighting, participation in informal economy; khaltura
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1857</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%98%D0%BB%D1%8C%D1%8F_%D0%92%D0%B0%D1%81%D0%B8%D0%BB%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87_%D0%A1%D0%B5%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%B2%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B2" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Илья Васильевич Селиванов">илья́ васи́льевич селива́нов</a></span>,  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">провинціа́льныя воспомина́нія. <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:записка.html>запи́сок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудак.html>чудака́</a></span></cite>, Moscow, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=R80NAAAAIAAJamp;pg=PA67">pages 67–68</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">стря́пчйі<sup style="font-style:normal">[<i>sic</i>]</sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоже.html>то́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> зналъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> испра́вникъ <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жный</a> человѣ́къ; <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всюду.html>всю́ду</a>, гдѣ стря́пчему быва́етъ <b><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ра</a></b>, испра́вникъ мо́жетъ <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отнять.html>отня́ть</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Strjápčji<sup style="font-style:normal">[<i>sic</i>]</sup> tóže óčenʹ xorošó znal, što isprávnik jemú núžnyj čelově́k; što vsjúdu, gdě strjápčemu byvájet <b>xaltúra</b>, isprávnik móžet jejó u nevó otnjátʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The Stryapchiy knew well too, that he needs the Ispravnik; that everywhere where the Stryapchiy gets an <b>extra-earning</b>, the Ispravnik might take it away from him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  G Wylx (lyrics),  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пацан.html>пацаны́</a></span>”, in  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">Джизнь</span></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>По</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́те</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:культура.html>культу́ре</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учеба.html>учёбе</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:амур.html>аму́ре</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:физкультура.html>физкульту́ре</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ре</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> гламу́ре<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:пацан.html>пацаны́</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Po rabóte, po kulʹtúre, i v učóbe i v amúre<br />V fizkulʹtúre, i v <b>xaltúre</b>, i v glamúre<br />Pacaný</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In work, in culture, and in studies and in love<br />In sport, and in moonlighting, and in glamor<br />Boys</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>shoddy work (something intentionally done badly), botched job, bungled job; hack; a botch; a pot boiler; khaltura
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> September 17,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9A%D0%BE%D0%BD%D1%8F%D0%B5%D0%B2,_%D0%90%D0%BD%D0%B4%D1%80%D0%B5%D0%B9_%D0%AE%D1%80%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Коняев, Андрей Юрьевич">андре́й коня́ев</a></span>,  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невыносимый.html>невыноси́мая</a> втори́чность <a href = vnd.unilang:бытие.html>бытия́</a>. андре́й коня́ев <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ре</a>, алекса́ндре <a href = vnd.unilang:невский.html>не́вском</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> дели́рии</span>”, in  <cite>Lenta.ru</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://lenta.ru/columns/2011/09/17/jesus/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говоримый.html>говори́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>ро́дине</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a> бл*, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> что́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давно.html>давно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подозревать.html>подозрева́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чило</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вство</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круго́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сплошной.html>сплошна́я</a> втори́чность <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:халтура.html>халту́ра</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My že govorím o Ródine! No bl*, ja štó-to takóje užé davnó podozrevál, múčilo menjá čúvstvo, što krugóm splošnája vtoríčnostʹ i <b>xaltúra</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We're talking about the Motherland, you know! But f*ck, I have long suspected something like that, I had a hurting feeling that everything around is sheer secondariness and a <b>hack job</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халтурить.html>халту́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xaltúritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li>хибара, <a href = vnd.unilang:лачуга.html>лачу́га</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:конура.html>конура́</a> (<i>перен.</i>)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:халява.html>халя́ва</a> (16562)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">חָלָב</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khaláv</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">milk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халява.html>халя́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xaljáva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халява.html>халя́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халява.html>халя́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:халява.html>халя́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(old use)</i> bootleg, top of the boot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> freebie</li></ol>

***хам.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>хам</a> (11145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>Хам</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Xam</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> - biblical character.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>хам</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xam</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>ха́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>ха́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хам.html>ха́мов</a></b>)
